    PROCEDURE SaveUrl@4(UrlP@1000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      "Url Part 1" := COPYSTR(UrlP,1,MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 1"));
      "Url Part 2" := COPYSTR(UrlP,MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 1") + 1,MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 2"));
      "Url Part 3" := COPYSTR(UrlP,MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 1") + MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 2") + 1,MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 3"));
      "Url Part 4" := COPYSTR(UrlP,MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 1") + MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 2") + MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 3") + 1,MAXSTRLEN("Url Part 4"));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetUrl@5() RetValO : Text;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("Url Part 1");
      RetValO := "Url Part 1" + "Url Part 2" + "Url Part 3" + "Url Part 4";
      EXIT(RetValO);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END;

    END.

    LOCAL PROCEDURE TestExistingSetup@1();
    BEGIN
      NuGetRepo.RESET;
      NuGetClSetup.RESET;

      IF (NuGetRepo.COUNT <> 0) OR (NuGetClSetup.COUNT <> 0) THEN
        ERROR(Text001);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateRepo@9(CodeP@1000 : Code[20];Description@1001 : Text;UrlP@1002 : Text);
    BEGIN
      NuGetRepo.RESET;

      NuGetRepo.INIT;
      NuGetRepo.Code := CodeP;
      NuGetRepo.TESTFIELD(Code);
      NuGetRepo.Description := Description;
      NuGetRepo.Active := TRUE;
      NuGetRepo.SaveUrl(UrlP);
      NuGetRepo.INSERT(TRUE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateClientConfig@10(RepoCodeP@1000 : Code[20]);
    BEGIN
      NuGetClSetup.RESET;

      NuGetClSetup.INIT;
      NuGetClSetup."Primary Key" := '';
      NuGetClSetup."Default Server Code" := RepoCodeP;
      NuGetClSetup."Repository Dataset Max. Size" := 500;
      NuGetClSetup."Installation Subpath" := 'Add-ins\NuGet\';
      NuGetClSetup.INSERT(TRUE);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
  RDLDATA
  {
  }
}

  CODE

    VAR
      NuGetCliSetup@1001 : Record 83631;
      DotNetExceptionHandler@1007 : Codeunit 1291;
      PckRepoFact@1002 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.PackageRepositoryFactory";

    LOCAL PROCEDURE "***PUBLICS***"@2();

    END;

    PROCEDURE GetDefaultPackageInstallationPath@9() RetValO : Text;
    BEGIN
      NuGetCliSetup.GetSetup(TRUE);
      NuGetCliSetup.TESTFIELD("Installation Subpath");
      RetValO := GetPackageInstallationPath(NuGetCliSetup."Installation Subpath");
      EXIT(RetValO);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetPackageInstallationPath@8(SubpathP@1000 : Text) RetValO : Text;
    VAR
      AssL@1001 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Reflection.Assembly";
    BEGIN
      //AssL.GetExecutingAssembly().
      RetValO := APPLICATIONPATH + SubpathP;
      EXIT(RetValO);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetPackagesFromDefaultServer@6(VAR NgtPckgEntryP@1003 : Record 83635;VAR NgtPckgEntryVersionP@1002 : Record 83636;VAR NetPckgListP@1004 : DotNet "'System.Core, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Linq.IQueryable`1";PckFilterP@1000 : Text;LoadNextP@1100225000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      NgtSrvL@1001 : Record 83632;
    BEGIN
      NuGetCliSetup.GetSetup(TRUE);
      NuGetCliSetup.TESTFIELD("Default Server Code");

      GetPackagesByNgtSrvCode(NgtPckgEntryP,NgtPckgEntryVersionP,NetPckgListP,NuGetCliSetup."Default Server Code",PckFilterP,LoadNextP);
    END;

    [TryFunction]
    PROCEDURE GetPackagesByNgtSrvCode@5(VAR NgtPckgEntryP@1003 : Record 83635;VAR NgtPckgEntryVersionP@1004 : Record 83636;VAR NetPckgListP@1005 : DotNet "'System.Core, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Linq.IQueryable`1";NgtCodeP@1002 : Code[20];PckFilterP@1000 : Text;LoadNextP@1100225000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      NuGetRepoL@1001 : Record 83632;
      ExceptionL@1006 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Exception";
    BEGIN
      NuGetRepoL.GET(NgtCodeP);
      NuGetRepoL.TESTFIELD(Active,TRUE);

      IF NOT GetPackagesByUrl(NgtPckgEntryP,NgtPckgEntryVersionP,NetPckgListP,NuGetRepoL.GetUrl,PckFilterP,LoadNextP) THEN BEGIN
        DotNetExceptionHandler.Collect;
        ERROR(Text004,DotNetExceptionHandler.GetMessage)
      END;
    END;

    [TryFunction]
    PROCEDURE GetPackagesByUrl@3(VAR NgtPckgEntryP@1003 : Record 83635;VAR NgtPckgEntryVersionP@1008 : Record 83636;VAR NetPckgListP@1009 : DotNet "'System.Core, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Linq.IQueryable`1";RepoUrlP@1002 : Text;PckFilterP@1000 : Text;LoadNextP@1100225007 : Boolean);
    VAR
      PckL@1001 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.IPackage";
      VersionL@1006 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.SemanticVersion";
      NetStrL@1100225000 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.String";
      ObjL@1100225002 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Object";
      FrameworksL@1100225013 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Collections.Generic.List`1";
      WndL@1004 : Dialog;
      VarL@1100225009 : Variant;
      PckIdL@1100225004 : Text;
      PckId2L@1100225006 : Text;
      PckTitleL@1100225003 : Text;
      PckDescrL@1100225005 : Text;
      ExitWithNextPckIdL@1100225001 : Boolean;
      PckCounterL@1100225008 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      NuGetCliSetup.GetSetup(FALSE);

      IF (NOT LoadNextP) THEN BEGIN
        PckCounter := 0;

        IF (PckFilterP = '') THEN BEGIN
          InitRepoVariables(RepoUrlP);
        END ELSE BEGIN
          CreateAggregateRepo(AgrRepo);
        END;

        NgtPckgEntryP.RESET;
        NgtPckgEntryP.DELETEALL;

        NgtPckgEntryVersionP.RESET;
        NgtPckgEntryVersionP.DELETEALL;
      END;

      WndL.OPEN(Text001);

      IF ((NOT ISNULL(PckRepo)) OR (NOT ISNULL(AgrRepo))) THEN BEGIN

        IF (NOT LoadNextP) THEN BEGIN
          IF (PckFilterP = '') THEN BEGIN
            NetPckgList := PckRepo.GetPackages;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            InstantiateGenericList(FrameworksL,'System.String');
            NetPckgList := AgrRepo.Search(PckFilterP,FrameworksL,NuGetCliSetup."Allow Pre-releases");
          END;
          NetPckgListEnum := NetPckgList.GetEnumerator;
        END;

        IF (NOT ISNULL(NetPckgListEnum)) THEN BEGIN

          WHILE NetPckgListEnum.MoveNext DO BEGIN
            PckL := NetPckgListEnum.Current;

            PckCounter += 1;
            PckCounterL += 1;

            DebugTextToFile(FORMAT(PckCounterL),PckCounterL,'nugetlog.start');

            IF (ISNULL(PckL)) THEN
              ERROR('PckL is NULL');

            IF (ISNULL(PckL.Version)) THEN
              ERROR('PckL.Version is NULL');
            VersionL := PckL.Version;

            // To be able compare null/empty .Net string we need to convert it to NAV text variable.
            // Then we can compare it as en empty text.
            PckIdL := PckL.Id;
            IF (PckIdL = '') THEN
              ERROR('PckL.Id is NULL or empty');

            IF ((ExitWithNextPckIdL) AND (PckIdL <> PckId2L)) THEN BEGIN
              WndL.CLOSE;
              EXIT;
            END;

            PckTitleL := PckL.Title;
            PckDescrL := PckL.Description;

            NgtPckgEntryP.INIT;
            NgtPckgEntryP."Package ID" := COPYSTR(PckIdL,1,MAXSTRLEN(NgtPckgEntryP."Package ID"));
            IF (PckTitleL <> '') THEN BEGIN
              NgtPckgEntryP.Title := COPYSTR(PckTitleL,1,MAXSTRLEN(NgtPckgEntryP.Title));
            END;
            IF (PckDescrL <> '') THEN BEGIN
              NgtPckgEntryP.Description := COPYSTR(PckDescrL,1,MAXSTRLEN(NgtPckgEntryP.Description));
            END;
            IF NOT NgtPckgEntryP.INSERT THEN NgtPckgEntryP.MODIFY;

            NgtPckgEntryVersionP.INIT;
            NgtPckgEntryVersionP."Package ID" := NgtPckgEntryP."Package ID";
            NgtPckgEntryVersionP.Version := VersionL.ToNormalizedString;
            IF (PckTitleL <> '') THEN BEGIN
              NgtPckgEntryVersionP.Title := COPYSTR(PckTitleL,1,MAXSTRLEN(NgtPckgEntryVersionP.Title));
            END;
            IF (PckDescrL <> '') THEN BEGIN
              NgtPckgEntryVersionP.Description := COPYSTR(PckDescrL,1,MAXSTRLEN(NgtPckgEntryVersionP.Description));
            END;
            NgtPckgEntryVersionP."Pckg. List Index" := PckCounter;
            IF NOT NgtPckgEntryVersionP.INSERT THEN NgtPckgEntryVersionP.MODIFY;

            DebugTextToFile(FORMAT(PckCounterL),PckCounterL,'nugetlog.end');

            WndL.UPDATE(1,NgtPckgEntryP."Package ID");
            WndL.UPDATE(2,PckCounter);

            PckId2L := PckIdL;

            IF (NOT ExitWithNextPckIdL) THEN BEGIN
              IF (NuGetCliSetup."Repository Dataset Max. Size" > 0) AND
                 (PckCounterL >= NuGetCliSetup."Repository Dataset Max. Size")
              THEN BEGIN
                // Load all version entries of the package ID being processed right now.
                ExitWithNextPckIdL := TRUE;
              END;
            END;
          END;
        END;
      END;

      WndL.CLOSE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InstallPackage@7(PckgIdP@1001 : Text;DestPathP@1000 : Text);
    VAR
      AgrRepoL@1002 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.AggregateRepository";
    BEGIN
      TestRepVars();
      CreateAggregateRepo(AgrRepoL);
      //PckMgr := PckMgr.PackageManager(PckRepo,DestPathP);
      PckMgr := PckMgr.PackageManager(AgrRepoL,DestPathP);
      PckMgr.InstallPackage(PckgIdP);
    END;

    PROCEDURE InstallPackageVersion@12(PckgIdP@1001 : Text;VersionP@1002 : Text;DestPathP@1000 : Text);
    VAR
      VersionL@1003 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.SemanticVersion";
    BEGIN
      VersionL := VersionL.Parse(VersionP);
      InstallPackageVersion2(PckgIdP,VersionL,DestPathP);
    END;

    PROCEDURE InstallPackageVersion2@11(PckgIdP@1001 : Text;VersionP@1002 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.SemanticVersion";DestPathP@1000 : Text);
    VAR
      AgrRepoL@1003 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.AggregateRepository";
    BEGIN
      NuGetCliSetup.GetSetup(FALSE);

      TestRepVars();
      CreateAggregateRepo(AgrRepoL);
      //PckMgr := PckMgr.PackageManager(PckRepo,DestPathP);
      PckMgr := PckMgr.PackageManager(AgrRepoL,DestPathP);
      PckMgr.InstallPackage(PckgIdP,VersionP,FALSE,NuGetCliSetup."Allow Pre-releases");
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE "***PRIVATES***"@4();
    BEGIN
      // SECTION SEPARATOR
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitRepoVariables@1(RepoUrlP@1000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      PckRepo := PckRepoFact.Default.CreateRepository(RepoUrlP);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE TestRepVars@13();
    BEGIN
      IF ISNULL(PckRepo) THEN
        ERROR(Text002);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateAggregateRepo@10(VAR AgrRepoP@1000 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.AggregateRepository");
    VAR
      NuGetRepoL@1002 : Record 83632;
      NgtRepoListL@1001 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Collections.Generic.List`1";
      PckRepoFactL@1004 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.PackageRepositoryFactory";
      PckRepoL@1003 : DotNet "'NuGet.Core, Version=2.8.60717.93, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.NuGet.IPackageRepository";
    BEGIN
      //NgtRepoListL := NgtRepoListL.List;
      SimpleGenericInitializer(NgtRepoListL,PckRepoL);

      NuGetRepoL.SETRANGE(Active,TRUE);
      IF NuGetRepoL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT

          CLEAR(PckRepoL);
          CLEAR(PckRepoFactL);

          PckRepoL := PckRepoFactL.Default.CreateRepository(NuGetRepoL.GetUrl);

          NgtRepoListL.Add(PckRepoL);

        UNTIL NuGetRepoL.NEXT = 0;

      AgrRepoP := AgrRepoP.AggregateRepository(NgtRepoListL);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SimpleGenericInitializer@14(GenericP@1001 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Object";ObjP@1003 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Object");
    VAR
      TypeL@1000 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Type";
      ArrayL@1002 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Array";
      ActivatorL@1004 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Activator";
    BEGIN

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DebugTextToFile@1100225001(TextP@1100225000 : Text;IndexP@1100225003 : Integer;ExtensionP@1100225002 : Text);

      FileMgtL@1100225004 : Codeunit 419;
      ServerFileHelperL@1100225006 : DotNet "'mscorlib'.System.IO.File";

        EXIT;

      FileMgtL.DeleteServerFile(TmpFileL);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitDefaultSetupData@27(RepoCodeP@1002 : Code[20];UrlP@1003 : Text;DescriptionP@1004 : Text);
    VAR
      NuGetRespL@1000 : Record 83632;
      NuGetClientSetupL@1001 : Record 83631;
    BEGIN
      NuGetRespL.INIT;
      NuGetRespL.Code := RepoCodeP;
      NuGetRespL.Description := DescriptionP;
      NuGetRespL.Active := TRUE;
      NuGetRespL.SaveUrl(UrlP);
      NuGetRespL.INSERT;

      NuGetClientSetupL.INIT;
      NuGetClientSetupL."Default Server Code" := RepoCodeP;
      NuGetClientSetupL."Installation Subpath" := STRSUBSTNO('Add-ins\%1\',RepoCodeP);
      NuGetClientSetupL.INSERT;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

  {
    VAR
      NgtCliMgt@1000 : Codeunit 83631;
      NgtPckgList@1004 : DotNet "'System.Core, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Linq.IQueryable`1";

      Text001@1002 : TextConst 'ENU=Done!';
      SearchText@1100225000 : Text;
      xSearchText@1100225001 : Text;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InstallPackage@2();
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Description);
      NgtCliMgt.InstallPackage("Package ID",PckgDestPath);

      MESSAGE(Text001);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InstallPackageVersion@1();
    VAR
      VersionL@1000 : Text;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD(Description);

      VersionL := CurrPage.PckgVersionList.PAGE.GetVersionNo;
      NgtCliMgt.InstallPackageVersion("Package ID",VersionL,PckgDestPath);

      MESSAGE(Text001);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitPackageList@3(LoadNextP@1100225000 : Boolean);
    VAR
      NgtPckgEntryVersionTMPL@1000 : TEMPORARY Record 83636;
    BEGIN
      CurrPage.PckgVersionList.PAGE.SetSharedRec(NgtPckgEntryVersionTMPL);

      PckgDestPath := NgtCliMgt.GetDefaultPackageInstallationPath;
      NgtCliMgt.GetPackagesFromDefaultServer(Rec,NgtPckgEntryVersionTMPL,NgtPckgList,SearchText,LoadNextP);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE OnSearchTextChage@1100225000();
    BEGIN
      IF (SearchText = xSearchText) THEN
        EXIT;

      InitPackageList(FALSE);

      xSearchText := SearchText;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
